         # Design Specification for the Online Auction Web Application
         
         ## 1. Flask Routes Specification
         
         | Path | Function Name | HTTP Method | Template | Context Variables |
         |-------|----------------------|-------------|------------------|-------------------|
         | /dashboard | dashboard | GET | dashboard.html | featured_auctions: list of auction dicts |
         | /auction/catalog | auction_catalog | GET | catalog.html | auctions: list of auction dicts, categories: list of category dicts |
         | /auction/<int:auction_id> | auction_details | GET | auction_details.html | auction: dict, bid_history: list of bid dicts, highest_bid: float |
         | /auction/<int:auction_id>/place_bid | place_bid | GET, POST | place_bid.html | auction: dict, minimum_bid: float; POST form: bidder_name, bid_amount |
         | /bid/history | bid_history | GET | bid_history.html | bids: list of bid dicts, auction_filter: int optional |
         | /categories | categories | GET | categories.html | categories: list of category dicts |
         | /winners | winners | GET | winners.html | winners: list of winner dicts, filter_name: str optional |
         | /trending | trending_auctions | GET | trending.html | trending_auctions: list of auction dicts, time_range: str |
         | /status | status | GET | status.html | auctions: list of auction dicts, status_filter: str optional |
         
         ### Notes:
         - All dynamic route parameters are passed as ints.
         - POST route for placing bids accepts bidder_name and bid_amount in form data.
         - Filters in query parameters where indicated.
         
         ## 2. HTML Templates Specification
         
         ### 1. Dashboard (dashboard.html)
         - Title: Auction Dashboard
         - Elements:
           - Div id="dashboard-page"
           - Div id="featured-auctions" // displays featured auction items
           - Button id="browse-auctions-button" to navigate to /auction/catalog
           - Button id="view-bids-button" to navigate to /bid/history
           - Button id="view-trending-button" to navigate to /trending
         
         ### 2. Auction Catalog (catalog.html)
         - Title: Auction Catalog
         - Elements:
           - Div id="catalog-page"
           - Input id="search-input" type="text" for live search
           - Select id="category-filter" for category filtering
           - Div id="auction-cards" containing auction cards
           - Each auction card:
             - Button id="view-auction-button-{{ auction.auction_id }}" to /auction/{{ auction.auction_id }}
         
         ### 3. Auction Details (auction_details.html)
         - Title: Auction Details
         - Elements:
           - Div id="auction-details"
           - Div id="auction-title" showing auction.title
           - Div id="auction-description" for description
           - Div id="highest-bid" showing highest bid amount
           - Button id="place-bid-button" to /auction/{{ auction.auction_id }}/place_bid
         
         ### 4. Place Bid (place_bid.html)
         - Title: Place Bid
         - Elements:
           - Div id="place-bid-container"
           - Input id="bidder-name" type="text"
           - Input id="bid-amount" type="number" min={{ minimum_bid }} step="0.01"
           - Div id="minimum-bid" shows minimum bid amount
           - Button id="submit-bid-button" to submit form
         
         ### 5. Bid History (bid_history.html)
         - Title: Bid History
         - Elements:
           - Div id="bid-history-page"
           - Select id="filter-by-auction" to filter bids by auction
           - Table id="bids-table" with columns: Bid ID, Auction Name, Bidder, Amount, Time
           - Button id="back-to-dashboard" to /dashboard
         
         ### 6. Categories (categories.html)
         - Title: Auction Categories
         - Elements:
           - Div id="categories-page"
           - Div id="categories-list" with category cards
           - Each category card includes name, description, item count
           - Button on each category card to filter auctions by category
           - Button id="back-to-dashboard" to /dashboard
         
         ### 7. Winners (winners.html)
         - Title: Winning Items
         - Elements:
           - Div id="winners-container"
           - Div id="winners-list" with winner cards (item_name, winner_name, winning_bid)
           - Input id="filter-by-winner" to filter winners
           - Button id="back-to-dashboard" to /dashboard
         
         ### 8. Trending Auctions (trending.html)
         - Title: Trending Auctions
         - Elements:
           - Div id="trending-page"
           - Select id="time-range-filter" with options: "24 Hours", "All Time"
           - Auction list with buttons id="view-auction-button-{{ auction.auction_id }}"
           - Button id="back-to-dashboard" to /dashboard
         
         ### 9. Status Page (status.html)
         - Title: Auction Status
         - Elements:
           - Div id="status-page"
           - Select id="status-filter" with options "Open", "Closed", "Upcoming"
           - Table id="status-table" with auction details: name, current bid, time remaining
           - Button id="refresh-status-button"
           - Button id="back-to-dashboard" to /dashboard
         
         ## 3. Data Schemas
         
         ### Data files are pipe-separated (|) text files in the 'data' directory.
         
         ### auctions.txt
         | field          | type     | description                      |
         |----------------|----------|--------------------------------|
         | auction_id     | int      | Unique auction identifier       |
         | item_name      | string   | Name of the item                |
         | description    | string   | Item description                |
         | category       | string   | Item category                   |
         | starting_bid   | float    | Starting bid price              |
         | current_bid    | float    | Current highest bid             |
         | end_time       | datetime | Auction end time (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM) |
         | status         | string   | Auction status (Active/Closed) |
         | image_url      | string   | Filename of item image          |
         
         **Example line:**
         ```
         1|Vintage Leather Jacket|A well made vintage leather jacket|Clothing|30.00|50.00|2025-12-01 18:00|Active|leather_jacket.jpg
         ```
         
         ### bids.txt
         | field        | type     | description                       |
         |--------------|----------|---------------------------------|
         | bid_id       | int      | Unique bid identifier            |
         | auction_id   | int      | Auction the bid belongs to       |
         | bidder_name  | string   | Name of bidder                   |
         | bid_amount   | float    | Amount bid                      |
         | bid_time     | datetime | Time bid was placed (HH:MM)     |
         
         **Example line:**
         ```
         1|1|Alice|55.00|2025-11-30 15:45
         ```
         
         ### winners.txt
         | field         | type     | description                     |
         |---------------|----------|--------------------------------|
         | winner_id     | int      | Winner record ID                |
         | auction_id    | int      | Auction won                    |
         | item_name     | string   | Item name                      |
         | winner_name   | string   | Winner's name                  |
         | winning_bid   | float    | Winning bid amount             |
         | win_date      | datetime | Date of win (YYYY-MM-DD)       |
         
         **Example line:**
         ```
         1|3|Wooden Desk|Charlie Brown|110.00|2025-02-08
         ```
         
         ### categories.txt
         | field        | type    | description                    |
         |--------------|---------|--------------------------------|
         | category_id  | int     | Category ID                   |
         | category_name| string  | Name of category              |
         | description  | string  | Category description          |
         | item_count   | int     | Number of auctions in category|
         
         **Example line:**
         ```
         1|Electronics|Digital devices and gadgets|15
         ```
         
         ### items.txt
         | field        | type    | description                   |
         |--------------|---------|-------------------------------|
         | item_id      | int     | Item identifier               |
         | auction_id   | int     | Auction associated            |
         | item_name    | string  | Item name                    |
         | starting_price| float  | Starting price                |
         | category     | string  | Category                     |
         | description  | string  | Item description             |
         
         **Example line:**
         ```
         2|1|iPhone 14 Pro|500.00|Electronics|Latest model smartphone
         ```
         
         ## End of specification.

      File: /home/jun/0624/CaMP/results/Software-web-rebuttal/compound_timeout_300/OnlineAuction/compound_chaos/app.py

      Before (full content):
         from flask import Flask, render_template, request, redirect, url_for, abort, flash
         import os
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.secret_key = 'secret-key-for-session'
         
         data_dir = 'data'
         
         # Data loading functions
         
         def load_auctions():
             auctions = {}
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(data_dir, 'auctions.txt'), 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     lines = f.readlines()
                     for line in lines:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) < 7:
                             continue
                         id_ = parts[0]
                         auctions[id_] = {
                             'id': id_,
                             'title': parts[1],
                             'starting_price': float(parts[2]),
                             'category_id': parts[3],
                             'status': parts[4],
                             'seller': parts[5],
                             'description': parts[6],
                             'bids': []
                         }
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return auctions
         
         
         def load_categories():
             categories = {}
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(data_dir, 'categories.txt'), 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     lines = f.readlines()
                     for line in lines:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) < 2:
                             continue
                         categories[parts[0]] = parts[1]
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return categories
         
         
         def load_bids():
             bids = []
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(data_dir, 'bids.txt'), 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     lines = f.readlines()
                     for line in lines:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) < 4:
                             continue
                         bid = {
                             'id': parts[0],
                             'auction_id': parts[1],
                             'bidder': parts[2],
                             'amount': float(parts[3])
                         }
                         bids.append(bid)
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return bids
         
         
         # Load data once at startup
         auctions = load_auctions()
         categories = load_categories()
         bids = load_bids()
         
         # Distribute bids to auctions
         for bid in bids:
             auction = auctions.get(bid['auction_id'])
             if auction:
                 auction['bids'].append(bid)
         
         
         @app.route('/')
         def index():
             # Show auctions on homepage
             return render_template('index.html', auctions=auctions.values(), categories=categories)
         
         
         @app.route('/auction/<auction_id>')
         def auction_detail(auction_id):
             auction = auctions.get(auction_id)
             if not auction:
                 abort(404, description='Auction not found')
             return render_template('auction_detail.html', auction=auction, categories=categories)
         
         
         @app.route('/auction/<auction_id>/place_bid', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def place_bid(auction_id):
             auction = auctions.get(auction_id)
             if not auction:
                 abort(404, description='Auction not found')
             if auction['status'].lower() != 'open':
                 flash('This auction is not open for bidding.')
                 return redirect(url_for('auction_detail', auction_id=auction_id))
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 bidder = request.form.get('bidder', '').strip()
                 amount_str = request.form.get('amount', '').strip()
                 try:
                     amount = float(amount_str)
                 except ValueError:
                     flash('Invalid amount value.')
                     return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)
         
                 if not bidder:
                     flash('Bidder name is required.')
                     return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)
         
                 current_max_bid = max([bid['amount'] for bid in auction['bids']], default=auction['starting_price'])
                 if amount <= current_max_bid:
                     flash(f'Bid must be higher than current maximum bid ({current_max_bid}).')
                     return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)
         
                 # Add new bid
                 new_bid = {
                     'id': str(len(bids) + 1),
                     'auction_id': auction_id,
                     'bidder': bidder,
                     'amount': amount
                 }
                 bids.append(new_bid)
                 auction['bids'].append(new_bid)
         
                 # Save bids back to file
                 try:
                     with open(os.path.join(data_dir, 'bids.txt'), 'a', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                         f.write(f"{new_bid['id']}|{new_bid['auction_id']}|{new_bid['bidder']}|{new_bid['amount']}\n")
                 except Exception:
                     # Unable to save bid, remove from list to keep data consistent
                     bids.pop()
                     auction['bids'].pop()
                     flash('Failed to save bid. Please try again later.')
                     return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)
         
                 return redirect(url_for('auction_detail', auction_id=auction_id))
         
             return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)
         
         
         @app.route('/categories')
         def list_categories():
             return render_template('categories.html', categories=categories)
         
         
         @app.route('/category/<category_id>')
         def auctions_by_category(category_id):
             if category_id not in categories:
                 abort(404, description='Category not found')
             filtered_auctions = [a for a in auctions.values() if a['category_id'] == category_id]
             return render_template('category_auctions.html', auctions=filtered_auctions, category=categories[category_id])
         
         
         @app.route('/bid/history')
         def bid_history():
             # Safeguard to avoid internal server error if bids list is empty or malformed
             if not bids:
                 return render_template('bid_history.html', bids=[], auctions=auctions)
         
             # Show bid history sorted by bid id (assumed numeric)
             try:
                 bids_sorted = sorted(bids, key=lambda b: int(b['id']))
             except Exception:
                 bids_sorted = bids
         
             return render_template('bid_history.html', bids=bids_sorted, auctions=auctions)
         
         
         @app.route('/winners')
         def winners():
             winners_list = []
             for auction in auctions.values():
                 if auction['status'].lower() == 'closed' and auction['bids']:
                     max_bid = max(auction['bids'], key=lambda b: b['amount'])
                     winners_list.append({'auction': auction, 'winner_bid': max_bid})
             return render_template('winners.html', winners=winners_list)
         
         
         @app.route('/trending')
         def trending_auctions():
             # For simplicity, trending auctions are the ones with the most bids
             auctions_sorted = sorted(auctions.values(), key=lambda a: len(a['bids']), reverse=True)
             return render_template('trending.html', auctions=auctions_sorted[:10])
         
         
         @app.route('/status/<status_filter>')
         def status_filter(status_filter):
             filtered_auctions = [a for a in auctions.values() if a['status'].lower() == status_filter.lower()]
             return render_template('status.html', auctions=filtered_auctions, status=status_filter)
         
         
         # 404 error handler with simple message
         @app.errorhandler(404)
         def not_found(e):
             return render_template('404.html', message=e.description), 404
         
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True)

                         }
             except Exception:

             return auctions

         from flask import Flask, render_template, request, redirect, url_for, abort, flash
         import os
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.secret_key = 'your_secret_key_here'
         
         data_dir = 'data'
         
         # Functions to load data from files
         
         def load_auctions():
             auctions = {}
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(data_dir, 'auctions.txt'), 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 7:
                             continue
                         auction_id, title, starting_price, category_id, status, seller, description = parts
                         auctions[auction_id] = {
                             'id': auction_id,
                             'title': title,
                             'starting_price': float(starting_price),
                             'category_id': category_id,
                             'status': status,
                             'seller': seller,
                             'description': description,
                             'bids': []
                         }
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return auctions
         
         
         def load_categories():
             categories = {}
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(data_dir, 'categories.txt'), 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 2:
                             continue
                         category_id, name = parts
                         categories[category_id] = name
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return categories
         
         
         def load_bids():
             bids = []
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(data_dir, 'bids.txt'), 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 4:
                             continue
                         bid_id, auction_id, bidder, amount_str = parts
                         try:
                             amount = float(amount_str)
                         except ValueError:
                             continue
                         bids.append({
                             'id': bid_id,
                             'auction_id': auction_id,
                             'bidder': bidder,
                             'amount': amount
                         })
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return bids
         
         
         # Load all data at startup
         auctions = load_auctions()
         categories = load_categories()
         bids = load_bids()
         
         # Associate bids with auctions
         for bid in bids:
             auction = auctions.get(bid['auction_id'])
             if auction:
                 auction['bids'].append(bid)
         
         
         @app.route('/')
         def index():
             return render_template('index.html', auctions=auctions.values(), categories=categories)
         
         
         @app.route('/auction/<auction_id>')
         def auction_detail(auction_id):
             auction = auctions.get(auction_id)
             if not auction:
                 abort(404, description='Auction not found')
             return render_template('auction_detail.html', auction=auction, categories=categories)
         
         
         @app.route('/auction/<auction_id>/place_bid', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def place_bid(auction_id):
             auction = auctions.get(auction_id)
             if not auction:
                 abort(404, description='Auction not found')
         
             if auction['status'].lower() != 'open':
                 flash('This auction is not open for bidding.')
                 return redirect(url_for('auction_detail', auction_id=auction_id))
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 bidder = request.form.get('bidder', '').strip()
                 amount_str = request.form.get('amount', '').strip()
         
                 if not bidder:
                     flash('Bidder name is required.')
                     return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)
         
                 try:
                     amount = float(amount_str)
                 except ValueError:
                     flash('Invalid bid amount.')
                     return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)
         
                 current_max = max((bid['amount'] for bid in auction['bids']), default=auction['starting_price'])
         
                 if amount <= current_max:
                     flash(f'Bid must be higher than the current highest bid ({current_max}).')
                     return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)
         
                 # Add and save the new bid
                 new_id = str(len(bids) + 1)
                 new_bid = {
                     'id': new_id,
                     'auction_id': auction_id,
                     'bidder': bidder,
                     'amount': amount
                 }
         
                 bids.append(new_bid)
                 auction['bids'].append(new_bid)
         
                 try:
                     with open(os.path.join(data_dir, 'bids.txt'), 'a', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                         f.write(f"{new_id}|{auction_id}|{bidder}|{amount}\n")
                 except Exception:
                     bids.pop()
                     auction['bids'].pop()
                     flash('Failed to save bid. Please try again later.')
                     return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)
         
                 return redirect(url_for('auction_detail', auction_id=auction_id))
         
             return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)
         
         
         @app.route('/categories')
         def categories_view():
             return render_template('categories.html', categories=categories)
         
         
         @app.route('/category/<category_id>')
         def auctions_by_category(category_id):
             if category_id not in categories:
                 abort(404, description='Category not found')
             filtered_auctions = [a for a in auctions.values() if a['category_id'] == category_id]
             return render_template('category_auctions.html', auctions=filtered_auctions, category=categories[category_id])
         
         
         @app.route('/bid/history')
         def bid_history():
             try:
                 sorted_bids = sorted(bids, key=lambda b: int(b['id']))
             except Exception:
                 sorted_bids = bids
             return render_template('bid_history.html', bids=sorted_bids, auctions=auctions)
         
         
         @app.route('/winners')
         def winners_view():
             winners_list = []
             for auction in auctions.values():
                 if auction['status'].lower() == 'closed' and auction['bids']:
                     highest_bid = max(auction['bids'], key=lambda b: b['amount'])
                     winners_list.append({'auction': auction, 'winner_bid': highest_bid})
             return render_template('winners.html', winners=winners_list)
         
         
         @app.route('/trending')
         def trending_auctions():
             sorted_auctions = sorted(auctions.values(), key=lambda a: len(a['bids']), reverse=True)
             return render_template('trending.html', auctions=sorted_auctions[:10])
         
         
         @app.route('/status/<status_filter>')
         def status_filter_route(status_filter):
             filtered_auctions = [a for a in auctions.values() if a['status'].lower() == status_filter.lower()]
             return render_template('status.html', auctions=filtered_auctions, status=status_filter)
         
         
         @app.errorhandler(404)
         def not_found(error):
             message = getattr(error, 'description', 'Resource not found')
             return render_template('404.html', message=message), 404
         
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True)

                             'id': auction_id,
                             'title': title,
                             'starting_price': float(starting_price),
                             'category_id': category_id,
                             'status': status,
                             'seller': seller,
                             'description': description,
                             'bids': []
                         }
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return auctions
         
         def load_categories():
             categories = {}
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'categories.txt'), 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 2:
                             continue
                         category_id, category_name = parts
                         categories[category_id] = category_name
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return categories
         
         def load_bids():
             bids = []
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'bids.txt'), 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 4:
                             continue
                         bid_id, auction_id, bidder, amount_str = parts
                         try:
                             amount = float(amount_str)
                         except ValueError:
                             continue
                         bids.append({
                             'id': bid_id,
                             'auction_id': auction_id,
                             'bidder': bidder,
                             'amount': amount
                         })
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return bids
         
         # Load data only once at application start
         auctions = load_auctions()
         categories = load_categories()
         bids = load_bids()
         
         # Assign bids to their auctions
         for bid in bids:
             auction = auctions.get(bid['auction_id'])
             if auction:
                 auction['bids'].append(bid)
         
         @app.route('/')
         def index():
             return render_template('index.html', auctions=auctions.values(), categories=categories)
         
         @app.route('/auction/<auction_id>')
         def auction_detail(auction_id):
             auction = auctions.get(auction_id)
             if not auction:
                 abort(404, description='Auction not found')
             return render_template('auction_detail.html', auction=auction, categories=categories)
         
         @app.route('/auction/<auction_id>/place_bid', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def place_bid(auction_id):
             auction = auctions.get(auction_id)
             if not auction:
                 abort(404, description='Auction not found')
         
             if auction['status'].lower() != 'open':
                 flash('This auction is not open for bidding.')
                 return redirect(url_for('auction_detail', auction_id=auction_id))
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 bidder = request.form.get('bidder', '').strip()
                 amount_str = request.form.get('amount', '').strip()
         
                 if not bidder:
                     flash('Bidder name is required.')
                     return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)
         
                 try:
                     amount = float(amount_str)
                 except ValueError:
                     flash('Invalid bid amount.')
                     return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)
         
                 current_max = max((bid['amount'] for bid in auction['bids']), default=auction['starting_price'])
         
                 if amount <= current_max:
                     flash(f'Bid must be higher than the current highest bid ({current_max}).')
                     return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)
         
                 new_bid_id = str(len(bids) + 1)
                 new_bid = {
                     'id': new_bid_id,
                     'auction_id': auction_id,
                     'bidder': bidder,
                     'amount': amount
                 }
         
                 bids.append(new_bid)
                 auction['bids'].append(new_bid)
         
                 try:
                     with open(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'bids.txt'), 'a', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                         f.write(f"{new_bid_id}|{auction_id}|{bidder}|{amount}\n")
                 except Exception:
                     bids.pop()
                     auction['bids'].pop()
                     flash('Failed to save bid. Please try again later.')
                     return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)
         
                 return redirect(url_for('auction_detail', auction_id=auction_id))
         
             return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)
         
         @app.route('/categories')
         def categories_view():
             return render_template('categories.html', categories=categories)
         
         @app.route('/category/<category_id>')
         def auctions_by_category(category_id):
             if category_id not in categories:
                 abort(404, description='Category not found')
             filtered_auctions = [a for a in auctions.values() if a['category_id'] == category_id]
             return render_template('category_auctions.html', auctions=filtered_auctions, category=categories[category_id])
         
         @app.route('/bid/history')
         def bid_history():
             try:
                 sorted_bids = sorted(bids, key=lambda b: int(b['id']))
             except Exception:
                 sorted_bids = bids
             return render_template('bid_history.html', bids=sorted_bids, auctions=auctions)
         
         @app.route('/winners')
         def winners_view():
             winners_list = []
             for auction in auctions.values():
                 if auction['status'].lower() == 'closed' and auction['bids']:
                     highest_bid = max(auction['bids'], key=lambda b: b['amount'])
                     winners_list.append({'auction': auction, 'winner_bid': highest_bid})
             return render_template('winners.html', winners=winners_list)
         
         @app.route('/trending')
         def trending_auctions():
             sorted_auctions = sorted(auctions.values(), key=lambda a: len(a['bids']), reverse=True)
             return render_template('trending.html', auctions=sorted_auctions[:10])
         
         @app.route('/status/<status_filter>')
         def status_filter_route(status_filter):
             filtered_auctions = [a for a in auctions.values() if a['status'].lower() == status_filter.lower()]
             return render_template('status.html', auctions=filtered_auctions, status=status_filter)
         
         @app.errorhandler(404)
         def not_found(error):
             message = getattr(error, 'description', 'Resource not found')
             return render_template('404.html', message=message), 404
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True)

         # Flask Web Application Design Specification
         
         ## Overview
         This document outlines the design specifications for the Online Auction Flask web application. The application enables users to browse auctions, place bids, view bid history, and see winning items. No user login or authentication is required. The website shall start on the Dashboard page.
         
         ---
         
         ## Application Pages
         
         ### 1. Dashboard Page
         - **Page Title:** Auction Dashboard
         - **Purpose:** Main page displaying featured auctions with navigation options.
         - **Elements:**
           - Div container with ID `dashboard-container` displaying auction items.
           - Button with ID `view-auction-catalog-button` to navigate to Auction Catalog page.
           - Button with ID `view-bids-button` to view bid history page.
           - Button with ID `view-trending-button` to navigate to Trending Auctions page.
         
         ### 2. Auction Catalog Page
         - **Page Title:** Auction Catalog
         - **Purpose:** Displays all available auctions with search and category filters.
         - **Elements:**
           - Div with ID `auction-list` displaying auction cards.
           - Input with ID `search-input` for searching auctions by name, description or item.
           - Select dropdown with ID `category-filter` for filtering auctions by category.
           - Each auction card includes auction image, title, starting bid, and a button (`view-auction-button-{{auction_id}}`) to view auction details.
         
         ### 3. Auction Details Page
         - **Page Title:** Auction Details
         - **Purpose:** Detailed view of an auction item.
         - **Elements:**
           - Div container with ID `auction-details-container`.
           - Auction title div `auction-title`.
           - Description div `auction-description`.
           - Highest bid display div `highest-bid`.
           - Button with ID `place-bid-button` to open bid placement page.
         
         ### 4. Place Bid Page
         - **Page Title:** Place Bid
         - **Purpose:** Allows entering bid details for an auction.
         - **Elements:**
           - Div with ID `place-bid-container`.
           - Input with ID `bidder-name` for bidder's name.
           - Input with ID `bid-amount` for bid amount.
           - Div with ID `minimum-bid` showing the minimum bid required.
           - Button with ID `submit-bid-button` to submit the bid.
         
         ### 5. Bid History Page
         - **Page Title:** Bid History
         - **Purpose:** Displays detailed bids made by users.
         - **Elements:**
           - Table with bid details: bid ID, auction name, bidder, amount, timestamp.
           - Dropdown filter to filter bids by auction.
           - Button with ID `back-to-dashboard` to return to Dashboard.
         
         ### 6. Categories Page
         - **Page Title:** Auction Categories
         - **Purpose:** Displays all auction categories with descriptions.
         - **Elements:**
           - Div with ID `categories-container` listing categories.
           - Each category card includes name, description, and item count.
           - Button on each category card for viewing auctions in that category.
           - Button with ID `back-to-dashboard` to navigate back.
         
         ### 7. Winning Items Page
         - **Page Title:** Winning Items
         - **Purpose:** Displays winning bids for auctions.
         - **Elements:**
           - Div container `winners-list` showing winning bid cards with bidder name, item, and winning bid.
           - Input filter `filter-by-winner` to filter by winner name.
           - Button with ID `back-to-dashboard` to navigate back.
         
         ### 8. Trending Auctions Page
         - **Page Title:** Trending Auctions
         - **Purpose:** Displays most active auctions sorted by bid count.
         - **Elements:**
           - Div container `trending-page` listing trending auctions.
           - Dropdown `time-range-filter` to filter by time range (Last 24 Hours, All Time).
           - Buttons `view-auction-button-{{auction_id}}` for each auction to view details.
           - Button with ID `back-to-dashboard` to return.
         
         ### 9. Status Page
         - **Page Title:** Auction Status
         - **Purpose:** Provides status overview of all auctions (open, closed, upcoming).
         - **Elements:**
           - Div with ID `status-page` displaying auctions status.
           - Dropdown `status-filter` to filter auctions by status.
           - Table showing auction details with time remaining and highest bid.
           - Button with ID `refresh-status-button` to refresh data.
           - Button with ID `back-to-dashboard` to return.
         
         ---
         
         ## Flask Routes
         
         | Path | Function Name | HTTP Method | Template | Parameters Passed |
         |------|---------------|-------------|----------|-------------------|
         | /dashboard | dashboard | GET | dashboard.html | None |
         | /auction/catalog | auction_catalog | GET | catalog.html | None |
         | /auction/<int:auction_id> | auction_details | GET | auction_details.html | auction_id: int |
         | /auction/<int:auction_id>/place_bid | place_bid | GET, POST | place_bid.html | auction_id: int; POST form data: bidder_name (str), bid_amount (float) |
         | /bid/history | bid_history | GET | bid_history.html | Optional filter: auction_id (int) |
         | /categories | categories | GET | categories.html | None |
         | /winners | winners | GET | winners.html | None |
         | /trending | trending_auctions | GET | trending.html | Optional filter: time_range (str; "24h" or "all") |
         | /status | status | GET | status.html | Optional filter: status_filter (str; e.g., "Open", "Closed", "Upcoming") |
         
         ---
         
         ## Templates Specification
         
         Each page template will follow these specifications:
         
         - Consistent casing and types for all element IDs.
         - Navigation elements have correct button IDs and link to the correct routes/functions.
         - Elements include precise IDs as per page requirements.
         - Use proper semantic HTML elements (e.g., div, button, input, select, table).
         - Example IDs:
           - `view-auction-button-{{ auction.auction_id }}` for auction detail buttons on catalog and trending pages.
           - `place-bid-button` on auction detail page to navigate to bid page.
           - `back-to-dashboard` button on all pages to return quickly to the dashboard.
         
         ---
         
         ## Data Schemas
         
         All data files are pipe-delimited text files, fields are consistent and well-defined:
         
         ### auctions.txt
         - Fields: auction_id|title|description|category|starting_bid|current_bid|end_time|status|image
         - Types: int|str|str|str|float|float|datetime|str|str
         - Example:
           `1|Vintage Leather Jacket|A well made vintage leather jacket|Clothing|30.00|50.00|2025-12-01 18:00:00|Active|leather_jacket.jpg`
         
         ### bids.txt
         - Fields: bid_id|auction_id|bidder_name|bid_amount|bid_time
         - Types: int|int|str|float|datetime
         - Example:
           `1001|1|John Doe|55.00|2025-11-30 15:45:00`
         
         ### bid_history.txt
         - Same structure as bids.txt, records historical bids.
         
         ### winners.txt
         - Fields: winner_id|auction_id|item_name|winner_name|winning_bid|win_date
         - Types: int|int|str|str|float|datetime
         - Example:
           `1|3|Wooden Desk|Charlie Brown|110.00|2025-02-08`
         
         ### categories.txt
         - Fields: category_id|category_name|description|item_count
         - Types: int|str|str|int
         - Example:
           `1|Electronics|Digital devices|10`
         
         ### items.txt
         - Fields: item_id|auction_id|item_name|starting_price|category|description
         - Types: int|int|str|float|str|str
         - Example:
           `2|1|iPhone 14 Pro|500.00|Electronics|Latest model smartphone`
         
         ---
         
         ## Critical Success Criteria
         
         - 100% accurate implementation of all specified Flask routes and templates with precise IDs.
         - Frontend and backend functionality strictly adheres to user requirements.
         - No additional functionality beyond specification.
         - Clear, consistent naming conventions across routes, functions, IDs, and templates.
         - Output precisely matches this specification document named `design_spec.md`.
         
         ---
         
         End of Design Specification.

         # Design Specification for the Online Auction Web Application
         
         ## 1. Flask Routes Specification
         
         | Path | Function Name | HTTP Method | Template | Context Variables |
         |-------|----------------------|-------------|------------------|-------------------|
         | /dashboard | dashboard | GET | dashboard.html | featured_auctions: list of auction dicts |
         | /auction/catalog | auction_catalog | GET | catalog.html | auctions: list of auction dicts, categories: list of category dicts |
         | /auction/<int:auction_id> | auction_details | GET | auction_details.html | auction: dict, bid_history: list of bid dicts, highest_bid: float |
         | /auction/<int:auction_id>/place_bid | place_bid | GET, POST | place_bid.html | auction: dict, minimum_bid: float; POST form: bidder_name, bid_amount |
         | /bid/history | bid_history | GET | bid_history.html | bids: list of bid dicts, auction_filter: int optional |
         | /categories | categories | GET | categories.html | categories: list of category dicts |
         | /winners | winners | GET | winners.html | winners: list of winner dicts, filter_name: str optional |
         | /trending | trending_auctions | GET | trending.html | trending_auctions: list of auction dicts, time_range: str |
         | /status | status | GET | status.html | auctions: list of auction dicts, status_filter: str optional |
         
         ### Notes:
         - All dynamic route parameters are passed as ints.
         - POST route for placing bids accepts bidder_name and bid_amount in form data.
         - Filters in query parameters where indicated.
         
         ## 2. HTML Templates Specification
         
         ### 1. Dashboard (dashboard.html)
         - Title: Auction Dashboard
         - Elements:
           - Div id="dashboard-page"
           - Div id="featured-auctions" // displays featured auction items
           - Button id="browse-auctions-button" to navigate to /auction/catalog
           - Button id="view-bids-button" to navigate to /bid/history
           - Button id="view-trending-button" to navigate to /trending
         
         ### 2. Auction Catalog (catalog.html)
         - Title: Auction Catalog
         - Elements:
           - Div id="catalog-page"
           - Input id="search-input" type="text" for live search
           - Select id="category-filter" for category filtering
           - Div id="auction-cards" containing auction cards
           - Each auction card:
             - Button id="view-auction-button-{{ auction.auction_id }}" to /auction/{{ auction.auction_id }}
         
         ### 3. Auction Details (auction_details.html)
         - Title: Auction Details
         - Elements:
           - Div id="auction-details"
           - Div id="auction-title" showing auction.title
           - Div id="auction-description" for description
           - Div id="highest-bid" showing highest bid amount
           - Button id="place-bid-button" to /auction/{{ auction.auction_id }}/place_bid
         
         ### 4. Place Bid (place_bid.html)
         - Title: Place Bid
         - Elements:
           - Div id="place-bid-container"
           - Input id="bidder-name" type="text"
           - Input id="bid-amount" type="number" min={{ minimum_bid }} step="0.01"
           - Div id="minimum-bid" shows minimum bid amount
           - Button id="submit-bid-button" to submit form
         
         ### 5. Bid History (bid_history.html)
         - Title: Bid History
         - Elements:
           - Div id="bid-history-page"
           - Select id="filter-by-auction" to filter bids by auction
           - Table id="bids-table" with columns: Bid ID, Auction Name, Bidder, Amount, Time
           - Button id="back-to-dashboard" to /dashboard
         
         ### 6. Categories (categories.html)
         - Title: Auction Categories
         - Elements:
           - Div id="categories-page"
           - Div id="categories-list" with category cards
           - Each category card includes name, description, item count
           - Button on each category card to filter auctions by category
           - Button id="back-to-dashboard" to /dashboard
         
         ### 7. Winners (winners.html)
         - Title: Winning Items
         - Elements:
           - Div id="winners-container"
           - Div id="winners-list" with winner cards (item_name, winner_name, winning_bid)
           - Input id="filter-by-winner" to filter winners
           - Button id="back-to-dashboard" to /dashboard
         
         ### 8. Trending Auctions (trending.html)
         - Title: Trending Auctions
         - Elements:
           - Div id="trending-page"
           - Select id="time-range-filter" with options: "24 Hours", "All Time"
           - Auction list with buttons id="view-auction-button-{{ auction.auction_id }}"
           - Button id="back-to-dashboard" to /dashboard
         
         ### 9. Status Page (status.html)
         - Title: Auction Status
         - Elements:
           - Div id="status-page"
           - Select id="status-filter" with options "Open", "Closed", "Upcoming"
           - Table id="status-table" with auction details: name, current bid, time remaining
           - Button id="refresh-status-button"
           - Button id="back-to-dashboard" to /dashboard
         
         ## 3. Data Schemas
         
         ### Data files are pipe-separated (|) text files in the 'data' directory.
         
         ### auctions.txt
         | field          | type     | description                      |
         |----------------|----------|--------------------------------|
         | auction_id     | int      | Unique auction identifier       |
         | item_name      | string   | Name of the item                |
         | description    | string   | Item description                |
         | category       | string   | Item category                   |
         | starting_bid   | float    | Starting bid price              |
         | current_bid    | float    | Current highest bid             |
         | end_time       | datetime | Auction end time (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM) |
         | status         | string   | Auction status (Active/Closed) |
         | image_url      | string   | Filename of item image          |
         
         **Example line:**
         ```
         1|Vintage Leather Jacket|A well made vintage leather jacket|Clothing|30.00|50.00|2025-12-01 18:00|Active|leather_jacket.jpg
         ```
         
         ### bids.txt
         | field        | type     | description                       |
         |--------------|----------|---------------------------------|
         | bid_id       | int      | Unique bid identifier            |
         | auction_id   | int      | Auction the bid belongs to       |
         | bidder_name  | string   | Name of bidder                   |
         | bid_amount   | float    | Amount bid                      |
         | bid_time     | datetime | Time bid was placed (HH:MM)     |
         
         **Example line:**
         ```
         1|1|Alice|55.00|2025-11-30 15:45
         ```
         
         ### winners.txt
         | field         | type     | description                     |
         |---------------|----------|--------------------------------|
         | winner_id     | int      | Winner record ID                |
         | auction_id    | int      | Auction won                    |
         | item_name     | string   | Item name                      |
         | winner_name   | string   | Winner's name                  |
         | winning_bid   | float    | Winning bid amount             |
         | win_date      | datetime | Date of win (YYYY-MM-DD)       |
         
         **Example line:**
         ```
         1|3|Wooden Desk|Charlie Brown|110.00|2025-02-08
         ```
         
         ### categories.txt
         | field        | type    | description                    |
         |--------------|---------|--------------------------------|
         | category_id  | int     | Category ID                   |
         | category_name| string  | Name of category              |
         | description  | string  | Category description          |
         | item_count   | int     | Number of auctions in category|
         
         **Example line:**
         ```
         1|Electronics|Digital devices and gadgets|15
         ```
         
         ### items.txt
         | field        | type    | description                   |
         |--------------|---------|-------------------------------|
         | item_id      | int     | Item identifier               |
         | auction_id   | int     | Auction associated            |
         | item_name    | string  | Item name                    |
         | starting_price| float  | Starting price                |
         | category     | string  | Category                     |
         | description  | string  | Item description             |
         
         **Example line:**
         ```
         2|1|iPhone 14 Pro|500.00|Electronics|Latest model smartphone
         ```
         
         ## End of specification.

         from flask import Flask, render_template, request, redirect, url_for, abort, flash
         import os
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.secret_key = 'secret-key-for-session'
         
         data_dir = 'data'
         
         # Data loading functions
         
         def load_auctions():
             auctions = {}
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(data_dir, 'auctions.txt'), 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     lines = f.readlines()
                     for line in lines:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) < 7:
                             continue
                         id_ = parts[0]
                         auctions[id_] = {
                             'id': id_,
                             'title': parts[1],
                             'starting_price': float(parts[2]),
                             'category_id': parts[3],
                             'status': parts[4],
                             'seller': parts[5],
                             'description': parts[6],
                             'bids': []
                         }
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return auctions
         
         
         def load_categories():
             categories = {}
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(data_dir, 'categories.txt'), 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     lines = f.readlines()
                     for line in lines:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) < 2:
                             continue
                         categories[parts[0]] = parts[1]
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return categories
         
         
         def load_bids():
             bids = []
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(data_dir, 'bids.txt'), 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     lines = f.readlines()
                     for line in lines:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) < 4:
                             continue
                         bid = {
                             'id': parts[0],
                             'auction_id': parts[1],
                             'bidder': parts[2],
                             'amount': float(parts[3])
                         }
                         bids.append(bid)
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return bids
         
         
         # Load data once at startup
         auctions = load_auctions()
         categories = load_categories()
         bids = load_bids()
         
         # Distribute bids to auctions
         for bid in bids:
             auction = auctions.get(bid['auction_id'])
             if auction:
                 auction['bids'].append(bid)
         
         
         @app.route('/')
         def index():
             # Show auctions on homepage
             return render_template('index.html', auctions=auctions.values(), categories=categories)
         
         
         @app.route('/auction/<auction_id>')
         def auction_detail(auction_id):
             auction = auctions.get(auction_id)
             if not auction:
                 abort(404, description='Auction not found')
             return render_template('auction_detail.html', auction=auction, categories=categories)
         
         
         @app.route('/auction/<auction_id>/place_bid', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def place_bid(auction_id):
             auction = auctions.get(auction_id)
             if not auction:
                 abort(404, description='Auction not found')
             if auction['status'].lower() != 'open':
                 flash('This auction is not open for bidding.')
                 return redirect(url_for('auction_detail', auction_id=auction_id))
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 bidder = request.form.get('bidder', '').strip()
                 amount_str = request.form.get('amount', '').strip()
                 try:
                     amount = float(amount_str)
                 except ValueError:
                     flash('Invalid amount value.')
                     return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)
         
                 if not bidder:
                     flash('Bidder name is required.')
                     return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)
         
                 current_max_bid = max([bid['amount'] for bid in auction['bids']], default=auction['starting_price'])
                 if amount <= current_max_bid:
                     flash(f'Bid must be higher than current maximum bid ({current_max_bid}).')
                     return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)
         
                 # Add new bid
                 new_bid = {
                     'id': str(len(bids) + 1),
                     'auction_id': auction_id,
                     'bidder': bidder,
                     'amount': amount
                 }
                 bids.append(new_bid)
                 auction['bids'].append(new_bid)
         
                 # Save bids back to file
                 try:
                     with open(os.path.join(data_dir, 'bids.txt'), 'a', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                         f.write(f"{new_bid['id']}|{new_bid['auction_id']}|{new_bid['bidder']}|{new_bid['amount']}\n")
                 except Exception:
                     # Unable to save bid, remove from list to keep data consistent
                     bids.pop()
                     auction['bids'].pop()
                     flash('Failed to save bid. Please try again later.')
                     return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)
         
                 return redirect(url_for('auction_detail', auction_id=auction_id))
         
             return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)
         
         
         @app.route('/categories')
         def list_categories():
             return render_template('categories.html', categories=categories)
         
         
         @app.route('/category/<category_id>')
         def auctions_by_category(category_id):
             if category_id not in categories:
                 abort(404, description='Category not found')
             filtered_auctions = [a for a in auctions.values() if a['category_id'] == category_id]
             return render_template('category_auctions.html', auctions=filtered_auctions, category=categories[category_id])
         
         
         @app.route('/bid/history')
         def bid_history():
             # Safeguard to avoid internal server error if bids list is empty or malformed
             if not bids:
                 return render_template('bid_history.html', bids=[], auctions=auctions)
         
             # Show bid history sorted by bid id (assumed numeric)
             try:
                 bids_sorted = sorted(bids, key=lambda b: int(b['id']))
             except Exception:
                 bids_sorted = bids
         
             return render_template('bid_history.html', bids=bids_sorted, auctions=auctions)
         
         
         @app.route('/winners')
         def winners():
             winners_list = []
             for auction in auctions.values():
                 if auction['status'].lower() == 'closed' and auction['bids']:
                     max_bid = max(auction['bids'], key=lambda b: b['amount'])
                     winners_list.append({'auction': auction, 'winner_bid': max_bid})
             return render_template('winners.html', winners=winners_list)
         
         
         @app.route('/trending')
         def trending_auctions():
             # For simplicity, trending auctions are the ones with the most bids
             auctions_sorted = sorted(auctions.values(), key=lambda a: len(a['bids']), reverse=True)
             return render_template('trending.html', auctions=auctions_sorted[:10])
         
         
         @app.route('/status/<status_filter>')
         def status_filter(status_filter):
             filtered_auctions = [a for a in auctions.values() if a['status'].lower() == status_filter.lower()]
             return render_template('status.html', auctions=filtered_auctions, status=status_filter)
         
         
         # 404 error handler with simple message
         @app.errorhandler(404)
         def not_found(e):
             return render_template('404.html', message=e.description), 404
         
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True)

                 return redirect(url_for('auction_detail', auction_id=auction_id))
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 bidder = request.form.get('bidder', '').strip()
                 amount_str = request.form.get('amount', '').strip()
         
                 try:
                     amount = float(amount_str)
                 except ValueError:
                     flash('Invalid bid amount.')
                     return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)
         
                 if not bidder:
                     flash('Bidder name is required.')
                     return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)
         
                 current_max = max([b['amount'] for b in auction['bids']], default=auction['starting_price'])
                 if amount <= current_max:
                     flash(f'Bid must be higher than current maximum ({current_max}).')
                     return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)
         
                 new_id = str(len(bids) + 1)
                 new_bid = {
                     'id': new_id,
                     'auction_id': auction_id,
                     'bidder': bidder,
                     'amount': amount
                 }
         
                 bids.append(new_bid)
                 auction['bids'].append(new_bid)
         
                 try:
                     with open(os.path.join(data_dir, 'bids.txt'), 'a', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                         f.write(f"{new_id}|{auction_id}|{bidder}|{amount}\n")
                 except Exception:
                     bids.pop()
                     auction['bids'].pop()
                     flash('Failed to save bid. Please try again later.')
                     return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)
         
                 return redirect(url_for('auction_detail', auction_id=auction_id))
         
             return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)
         
         
         @app.route('/categories')
         def categories_list():
             return render_template('categories.html', categories=categories)
         
         
         @app.route('/category/<category_id>')
         def auctions_by_category(category_id):
             if category_id not in categories:
                 abort(404, description='Category not found')
             filtered = [a for a in auctions.values() if a['category_id'] == category_id]
             return render_template('category_auctions.html', auctions=filtered, category=categories[category_id])
         
         
         @app.route('/bid/history')
         def bid_history():
             # Return bid history sorted by id integer
             try:
                 sorted_bids = sorted(bids, key=lambda x: int(x['id']))
             except Exception:
                 sorted_bids = bids
             return render_template('bid_history.html', bids=sorted_bids, auctions=auctions)
         
         
         @app.route('/winners')
         def winners():
             winners_list = []
             for auction in auctions.values():
                 if auction['status'].lower() == 'closed' and auction['bids']:
                     winner_bid = max(auction['bids'], key=lambda b: b['amount'])
                     winners_list.append({'auction': auction, 'winner_bid': winner_bid})
             return render_template('winners.html', winners=winners_list)
         
         
         @app.route('/trending')
         def trending():
             # Sort by number of bids descending and limit to top 10
             sorted_auctions = sorted(auctions.values(), key=lambda a: len(a['bids']), reverse=True)
             return render_template('trending.html', auctions=sorted_auctions[:10])
         
         
         @app.route('/status/<status_filter>')
         def status_filter_route(status_filter):
             filtered = [a for a in auctions.values() if a['status'].lower() == status_filter.lower()]
             return render_template('status.html', auctions=filtered, status=status_filter)
         
         
         @app.errorhandler(404)
         def handle_404(err):
             message = getattr(err, 'description', 'Resource not found')
             return render_template('404.html', message=message), 404
         
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True)

         from flask import Flask, render_template, request, redirect, url_for, abort, flash
         import os
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.secret_key = 'your_secret_key_here'
         
         data_dir = 'data'
         
         # Functions to load data from files
         
         def load_auctions():
             auctions = {}
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(data_dir, 'auctions.txt'), 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 7:
                             continue
                         auction_id, title, starting_price, category_id, status, seller, description = parts
                         auctions[auction_id] = {
                             'id': auction_id,
                             'title': title,
                             'starting_price': float(starting_price),
                             'category_id': category_id,
                             'status': status,
                             'seller': seller,
                             'description': description,
                             'bids': []
                         }
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return auctions
         
         
         def load_categories():
             categories = {}
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(data_dir, 'categories.txt'), 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 2:
                             continue
                         category_id, name = parts
                         categories[category_id] = name
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return categories
         
         
         def load_bids():
             bids = []
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(data_dir, 'bids.txt'), 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 4:
                             continue
                         bid_id, auction_id, bidder, amount_str = parts
                         try:
                             amount = float(amount_str)
                         except ValueError:
                             continue
                         bids.append({
                             'id': bid_id,
                             'auction_id': auction_id,
                             'bidder': bidder,
                             'amount': amount
                         })
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return bids
         
         
         # Load all data at startup
         auctions = load_auctions()
         categories = load_categories()
         bids = load_bids()
         
         # Associate bids with auctions
         for bid in bids:
             auction = auctions.get(bid['auction_id'])
             if auction:
                 auction['bids'].append(bid)
         
         
         @app.route('/')
         def index():
             return render_template('index.html', auctions=auctions.values(), categories=categories)
         
         
         @app.route('/auction/<auction_id>')
         def auction_detail(auction_id):
             auction = auctions.get(auction_id)
             if not auction:
                 abort(404, description='Auction not found')
             return render_template('auction_detail.html', auction=auction, categories=categories)
         
         
         @app.route('/auction/<auction_id>/place_bid', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def place_bid(auction_id):
             auction = auctions.get(auction_id)
             if not auction:
                 abort(404, description='Auction not found')
         
             if auction['status'].lower() != 'open':
                 flash('This auction is not open for bidding.')
                 return redirect(url_for('auction_detail', auction_id=auction_id))
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 bidder = request.form.get('bidder', '').strip()
                 amount_str = request.form.get('amount', '').strip()
         
                 if not bidder:
                     flash('Bidder name is required.')
                     return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)
         
                 try:
                     amount = float(amount_str)
                 except ValueError:
                     flash('Invalid bid amount.')
                     return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)
         
                 current_max = max((bid['amount'] for bid in auction['bids']), default=auction['starting_price'])
         
                 if amount <= current_max:
                     flash(f'Bid must be higher than the current highest bid ({current_max}).')
                     return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)
         
                 # Add and save the new bid
                 new_id = str(len(bids) + 1)
                 new_bid = {
                     'id': new_id,
                     'auction_id': auction_id,
                     'bidder': bidder,
                     'amount': amount
                 }
         
                 bids.append(new_bid)
                 auction['bids'].append(new_bid)
         
                 try:
                     with open(os.path.join(data_dir, 'bids.txt'), 'a', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                         f.write(f"{new_id}|{auction_id}|{bidder}|{amount}\n")
                 except Exception:
                     bids.pop()
                     auction['bids'].pop()
                     flash('Failed to save bid. Please try again later.')
                     return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)
         
                 return redirect(url_for('auction_detail', auction_id=auction_id))
         
             return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)

         from flask import Flask, render_template, request, redirect, url_for, abort, flash
         import os
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.secret_key = 'your_secret_key_here'
         
         DATA_DIR = 'data'
         
         # Data loading helper functions
         def load_auctions():
             auctions = {}
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'auctions.txt'), 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 7:
                             continue
                         auction_id, title, starting_price, category_id, status, seller, description = parts
                         auctions[auction_id] = {
                             'id': auction_id,
                             'title': title,
                             'starting_price': float(starting_price),
                             'category_id': category_id,
                             'status': status,
                             'seller': seller,
                             'description': description,
                             'bids': []
                         }
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return auctions
         
         def load_categories():
             categories = {}
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'categories.txt'), 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 2:
                             continue
                         category_id, category_name = parts
                         categories[category_id] = category_name
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return categories
         
         def load_bids():
             bids = []
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'bids.txt'), 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 4:
                             continue
                         bid_id, auction_id, bidder, amount_str = parts
                         try:
                             amount = float(amount_str)
                         except ValueError:
                             continue
                         bids.append({
                             'id': bid_id,
                             'auction_id': auction_id,
                             'bidder': bidder,
                             'amount': amount
                         })
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return bids
         
         # Load data only once at application start
         auctions = load_auctions()
         categories = load_categories()
         bids = load_bids()
         
         # Assign bids to their auctions
         for bid in bids:
             auction = auctions.get(bid['auction_id'])
             if auction:
                 auction['bids'].append(bid)
         
         @app.route('/')
         def index():
             return render_template('index.html', auctions=auctions.values(), categories=categories)
         
         @app.route('/auction/<auction_id>')
         def auction_detail(auction_id):
             auction = auctions.get(auction_id)
             if not auction:
                 abort(404, description='Auction not found')
             return render_template('auction_detail.html', auction=auction, categories=categories)
         
         @app.route('/auction/<auction_id>/place_bid', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def place_bid(auction_id):
             auction = auctions.get(auction_id)
             if not auction:
                 abort(404, description='Auction not found')
         
             if auction['status'].lower() != 'open':
                 flash('This auction is not open for bidding.')
                 return redirect(url_for('auction_detail', auction_id=auction_id))
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 bidder = request.form.get('bidder', '').strip()
                 amount_str = request.form.get('amount', '').strip()
         
                 if not bidder:
                     flash('Bidder name is required.')
                     return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)
         
                 try:
                     amount = float(amount_str)
                 except ValueError:
                     flash('Invalid bid amount.')
                     return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)

                 if amount <= current_max:
                     flash(f'Bid must be higher than the current highest bid ({current_max}).')
                     return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)

         @app.route('/categories')
         def categories_view():
             return render_template('categories.html', categories=categories)
         
         @app.route('/category/<category_id>')
         def auctions_by_category(category_id):
             if category_id not in categories:
                 abort(404, description='Category not found')
             filtered_auctions = [a for a in auctions.values() if a['category_id'] == category_id]
             return render_template('category_auctions.html', auctions=filtered_auctions, category=categories[category_id])
         
         @app.route('/bid/history')
         def bid_history():
             try:
                 sorted_bids = sorted(bids, key=lambda b: int(b['id']))
             except Exception:
                 sorted_bids = bids
             return render_template('bid_history.html', bids=sorted_bids, auctions=auctions)
         
         @app.route('/winners')
         def winners_view():
             winners_list = []
             for auction in auctions.values():
                 if auction['status'].lower() == 'closed' and auction['bids']:
                     highest_bid = max(auction['bids'], key=lambda b: b['amount'])
                     winners_list.append({'auction': auction, 'winner_bid': highest_bid})
             return render_template('winners.html', winners=winners_list)
         
         @app.route('/trending')
         def trending_auctions():
             sorted_auctions = sorted(auctions.values(), key=lambda a: len(a['bids']), reverse=True)
             return render_template('trending.html', auctions=sorted_auctions[:10])
         
         @app.route('/status/<status_filter>')
         def status_filter_route(status_filter):
             filtered_auctions = [a for a in auctions.values() if a['status'].lower() == status_filter.lower()]
             return render_template('status.html', auctions=filtered_auctions, status=status_filter)
         
         @app.errorhandler(404)
         def not_found(error):
             message = getattr(error, 'description', 'Resource not found')
             return render_template('404.html', message=message), 404
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True)
